***вареник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вареник.html>варе́ник</a> (29823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареник.html>варе́ник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">varénik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареник.html>варе́ника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареник.html>варе́ники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареник.html>варе́ников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a varenik/varenyk; a single vareniki/varenyky dumpling</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This word is more commonly used in the plural, where it refers to the dish itself.</li>
<li>The dish is considered Ukrainian but Russians make it quite often and consider it their own.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">варе́ничная</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">varéničnaja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vareniki/varenyky restaurant</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вареный.html>варёный</a> (8476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ёный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареный.html>варёный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">varjónyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>boiled, cooked by boiling <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a food</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вареный.html>варёное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйцо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>varjónoje</b> jajcó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">boiled egg</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Short forms <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареный.html>варён</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varjón</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареный.html>варёна</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varjóna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареный.html>варёно</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varjóno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареный.html>варёны</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varjóny</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> exist theoretically, but are usually avoided due to ambiguity with the (possibly colloquial) short forms of the past passive participle <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">варённый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***варенье.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:варенье.html>варе́нье</a> (6521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́нье</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énʹje</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варенье.html>варе́нье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">varénʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варенье.html>варе́нья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варенье.html>варе́нья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варенье.html>варе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>jam, varenye, murabba (<i>food; usually not as thick as</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:джем.html>джем</a>, <i>and with whole pieces of fruit or berry</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:варенье.html>варе́нье</a> should not be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">варе́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is a process of cooking by boiling.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нье</b>

Зализняка) |  <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:художественный.html>худо́жественной</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:особенно.html>осо́бенно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поэтический.html>поэти́ческой</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:речь.html>ре́чи</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:допустимый.html>допусти́ма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> предл. пад. ед. ч. <i>варе́ньи</i>.

***варить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a> (1743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*variti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to burn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">varítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сварить.html>свари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to cook, to boil</li>
<li>to brew <i>(beer)</i></li>
<li>to found, to weld</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The participle <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>ва́ренный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">várennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is considered to be the "official" past passive participle of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></b>. But its related adjective <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вареный.html>варёный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varjónyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is also derived from another "older" past passive participle of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></b>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">

<p><b>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:сварить.html>свари́ть</a>.

<p><b>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вар-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вар.html>ва́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:варьировать.html>варьи́ровать</a> (30692)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***варяг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:варяг.html>варя́г</a> (23203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">варѧгъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varęgŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">væringi</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> The figurative sense stems from the legendary summoning of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rurik" class="extiw" title="w:Rurik">Rurik</a> and the Varangians by the East Slavs.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варяг.html>варя́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">varjág</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варяг.html>варя́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варяг.html>варя́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варяг.html>варя́гов</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">варя́жка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Varangian, Viking</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">modern use</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an outsider or foreigner brought in to lead or help an organization or company, e.g. local bodies of state administration or a sports team
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зачем.html>Заче́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приглашать.html>приглаша́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:варяг.html>варя́га</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:специалист.html>специали́ст</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Začem nam priglašatʹ <b>varjaga</b>, jesli jestʹ svoj specialist?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Why should we invite an <b>outsider</b> if we have our own specialist?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ря́г</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
<a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:архаичный.html>архаи́чный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 3a(2): <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>. (<a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>) мн. <a href = vnd.unilang:варяг.html>варя́г</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:например.html>Наприме́р</a>: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>Из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:варяг.html>варя́г</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грек.html>гре́ки</a></i>.

***вата.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́та</a> (7651)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Watte</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ouate</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">váta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>absorbent cotton, cotton wool, wadding, batting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>váte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">wadded, padded</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пальто.html>пальто́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">palʹtó na <b>váte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">wadded coat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">cloth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> drugstore cotton</li>
<li>glass wool</li></ol>

***ватага.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ватага.html>вата́га</a> (23117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>A <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> borrowing with a sense development “tent, family” → “group of people”. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">otağ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватага.html>вата́га</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vatága</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватага.html>вата́ги</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватага.html>вата́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватага.html>вата́г</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gang (big, noisy group of people)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гурьба.html>гурьба́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gurʹbá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кодла.html>ко́дла</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kódla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***ватник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ватник.html>ва́тник</a> (9162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">váta</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cotton wool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Fotothek_df_ps_0000630_002_Tiere_%5E_V%C3%B6gel_%5E_Tauben_%5E_F%C3%BCtternde.jpg/220px-Fotothek_df_ps_0000630_002_Tiere_%5E_V%C3%B6gel_%5E_Tauben_%5E_F%C3%BCtternde.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="266" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Fotothek_df_ps_0000630_002_Tiere_%5E_V%C3%B6gel_%5E_Tauben_%5E_F%C3%BCtternde.jpg/330px-Fotothek_df_ps_0000630_002_Tiere_%5E_V%C3%B6gel_%5E_Tauben_%5E_F%C3%BCtternde.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/11/Fotothek_df_ps_0000630_002_Tiere_%5E_V%C3%B6gel_%5E_Tauben_%5E_F%C3%BCtternde.jpg/440px-Fotothek_df_ps_0000630_002_Tiere_%5E_V%C3%B6gel_%5E_Tauben_%5E_F%C3%BCtternde.jpg 2x" data-file-width="677" data-file-height="820" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:ватник.html>ва́тник</a> (1)</div></div></div>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватник.html>ва́тник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vátnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватник.html>ва́тника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватник.html>ва́тники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватник.html>ва́тников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quilted jacket</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> neologism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sovok, over-zealous extremely patriotic Russian person, the term was popularised by <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://vk.com">VKontakte</a> and <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.livejournal.com/">LIVEJOURNAL</a> and the Russian opposition in general</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The term (2) is considered Russophobic by many Russians.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">quilted jacket</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фуфайка.html>фуфа́йка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">fufájka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:телогрейка.html>телогре́йка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">telogréjka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">an over-patriotic Russian/Soviet citizen</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совок.html>сово́к</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sovók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:портянка.html>портя́нка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">portjánka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:никнуть.html>ни́к</a></b>

***ватный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ватный.html>ва́тный</a> (8383)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вата.html>ва́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">váta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватный.html>ва́тный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vátnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cotton wool, batting; wadded, quilted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ватный.html>ва́тный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:халат.html>хала́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vátnyj</b> xalát</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>cotton wool</b> bathrobe</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of limbs</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> powerless</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***ватрушка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ватрушка.html>ватру́шка</a> (31688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>The origin is unclear. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Iranian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Iranian language">Proto-Iranian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ira-pro">*ātr-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ira-pro">*ātar-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. 
Probably, from the info-iranian source through From Proto-Albanian <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Albanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Albanian language">Proto-Albanian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sqj-pro">*ōtar</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватрушка.html>ватру́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vatrúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватрушка.html>ватру́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватрушка.html>ватру́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватрушка.html>ватру́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Vatrushka.jpg/220px-Vatrushka.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Vatrushka.jpg/330px-Vatrushka.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Vatrushka.jpg/440px-Vatrushka.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="768" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><a href = vnd.unilang:ватрушка.html>ватру́шка</a></div></div></div>
<ol><li>vatrushka (a sort of small, round cottage cheese-filled pastry)</li>
<li>a round, inflatable snow saucer</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>ва<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тереть.html>тру́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-ватрушк-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вафель-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>вафля́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vafljá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вафля.html>вафли́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вафля.html>вафли́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вафля.html>вафле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> snot, spit</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> criminal jargon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cum, jizz, ejaculate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mythical flying dick; by extension, any flying object with an elongated shape, such as a Zeppelin
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вафля.html>вафли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vafli lovítʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hold the mouth open too long</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to catch flying dicks</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ва́ф<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ля.html>ля</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 2*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-вафл-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-я</b>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вахта.html>ва́хта</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">váxta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вахтенный.html>ва́хтенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">váxtennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> watch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вахтенный.html>ва́хтенный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:журнал.html>журна́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>váxtennyj</b> žurnál</i> ― <span class="e-translation">ship's log, logbook</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вахтенный.html>ва́хтенный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">váxtennyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вахтенный.html>ва́хтенного</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вахтенный.html>ва́хтенные</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вахтенный.html>ва́хтенных</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вахтенный.html>ва́хтенная</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> guard, watchman, sailor on duty</li></ol>
